10/14/22, 12:49 PM - Pupul '21: It's time for Hyderabad’s biggest and largest student-run Hackathon, Megathon. Megathon is a 24 hour hackathon with participants from all over the country, making it a wonderful platform to interact and collaborate with fellow participants as well as industry experts. Registrations are open right now. 
We, at E-cell IIIT Hyderabad are excited to bring to you a whole range of fun and challenging events to tickle the mind and bring people together to crack mind-boggling tech-based problems with a bit of entrepreneurial flair.  

Winners of the challenges have the chance to attend startup bootcamp at CIE-one of the largest academic incubators in India and to work on their ideas with mentors from esteemed companies. 

Give yourself a chance to come up with innovative solutions to real-world issues and transpose ideas from the drawing-board to the board room. Do not miss out on the opportunity to crack out the big-guns and take risks, as every entrepreneur says, “The biggest risk is to not take risks”. 

Participation is welcome from colleges from all over India. Scan the QR code on the poster or go to megathon.in for registering. 

Exclusive OFFER  Students discount offer: Use the coupon code "EARLYBIRD" for 50% off

11/1/22, 9:37 PM - Vighnesh Sreepathi'21: Dear friends, prakriti is back with another interesting event and this is our first techy event this year,
11/1/22, 9:37 PM - Vighnesh Sreepathi'21: Making of Soil Moisture Sensors. 
Measuring soil moisture is essential for agricultural applications since it allows farmers to manage their irrigation systems better. It is also significantly vital in erosion studies and research. This is an excellent opportunity for you all to make a prototype of the Soil Moisture Sensor and be part of the excitement. We'd love to have you all participate and win exciting prizes.
Further details of the event :
1. You can build any soil moisture sensor you like. We'll be even more delighted to get new prototypes with some advancements.
2. The submission should be in the form of a video presenting the making of the sensor. It's alright if it does not include the entire process. The video must be 2 min or longer. You are also required to submit some photos of the making.
3. You have to submit a description (report) of the working procedure and the components involved, or you can include them in the video. You can mention any advancements or suggestions also.
4. You can approach the EE Lab/Central Workshop for the required components.
5. To get a basic understanding of how to make these sensors do check out this video: https://youtu.be/e6CBy9TMIj0
 
This is an Online Event. Submit your Entries in this form.

The Deadline for the event is 5th Nov 2021.
Prize Money :
1st Place: Rs.1500/-
2nd Place: Rs.1000/-
3rd Place: Rs.500/-

As part of the Ministry of External Affairs' India@75:Videsh Niti Distinguished Lecture Series, former Ambassador Bhaswati Mukherjee will deliver a lecture at IIT Hyderabad on 4th November. The details of the talk and the venue are given below:

Speaker: Ambassador Bhaswati Mukherjee
Date: 4th November 2022 (Friday)
Time : 14:30 - 15:30;
Venue: B Block 110
Topic :  ' India and the G 20 Presidency: its priorities and challenges, with special focus on the Russia Ukraine Conflict'

As India will be assuming the Presidency of the G 20 on 1st December 22, the talk will be quite interesting and informative.

Ambassador Bhaswati Mukherjee  has vas experience on foreign policy and some of her important assignments are:

1. Ambassador of India to the Netherlands, the Hague during 31 July 2010 to 30    June 2013
2. Ambassador/Permanent Representative 20 September 2004 to 30 June 2010 of India to UNESCO, Paris.
3. Delivering Lectures at Sushma Swaraj Foreign Service Institute and Universities in India and abroad. Topics include disarmament and strategic issues, challenges emerging from use of chemical weapons, India’s relations with its neighbours, India and EU, as well as Diaspora, soft power and India’s cultural and civilizational heritage.
4. She Inscribed the Indentured Labour Route Project for UNESCO and Government of Mauritius on the World Heritage List.
 

5. She was a Senior Expert Consultant to DFID.

 

6. She was a Senior Consultant to MGIEP, UNESCO.

 

7. Best-selling Author and TV commentator.

Presently authoring “Indenture and its Route: a Relentless Quest for Identity” for Rupa Publications

12/18/22, 5:33 PM - Abhay Biomed: *Inter IIT High Prep Problem Statement: Drona Aviation (Aerial Robotics) Team Selection*

Hey all!

We have the second problem statement released for this year's Inter IIT Tech Meet. The problem statement is from the Aerial Robotics domain.

*Problem Statement:*

You may have a look at the problem statement in the link given below.

The problem statement is about *"Drona Aviation: Pluto Drone Swarm Challenge"*

_Problem Statement Link:_ https://interiit-tech.org/images/ps/High_Drona.pdf

*Team Selection:*

If you think you would be able to contribute in solving this problem statement and have previous experience which might be useful for us, then please fill this form. 

A previous experience in the following areas would be really handy:
1. Basics of drones (propellers, motors, pitch, yaw, roll, etc.,)
2. ROS Kinetics
3. OpenCV

_Form Link:_ https://forms.gle/cEfmqU3FrA9rcvYZA

_Deadline to fill the form:_ 5:00 PM, 19th December 2022.

*Logistics:*

1. The maximum team size for this problem statement is 10. 
2. There is no mid-term evaluation.
3. Final Evaluation will be tentatively on 10th February 2023.

2/25/23, 3:36 PM - Manoj Kumar ES: *Epoch-TL: Vision Quest Hackathon*

Hey all!

We are proud to announce that Epoch is collaborating with TL to organise a Machine Learning Hackathon open to the student community. So ML enthusiasts, put on your thinking hats, and start "networking" away. [ reference to Neural Networks:) ] 

You can find the PS here.

Link: https://docs.google.com/document/d/1fjYSDLiyjajfUuN6uehUYKx39h-_jIzd9TE3wr2FLeY/edit?usp=sharing

Now hold up! We don't want to spoil the entire thing now, do we? The doc shared above is merely a general overview of how the PS would be. We will have an elaborate presentation of the PS, with all the finer details for the ones who register.

So, what are you waiting for? Register here.

Link: https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSfK3Cs6Qp_GOG9ek6z5fSriI_NhnwXjPTKMI5E0Ccs40bvTnA/viewform?usp=sf_link

 *Deadline: 11:59 PM, 1st March 2023* 

We will have *cash prizes of up to Rs. 5000* for the winners. 

Note that we are also in discussion with Professors to guide this project, so the one with the best model will get a chance to work on the end-to-end implementation of this entire system, under the guidance of a Prof.

P.S. We know B.Tech freshers might be feeling a bit intimidated by the technical details of this problem statement, and wondering if they have what it takes to win. To put these fears to rest, freshers who impress us with their work will get a *special prize on behalf of Epoch and TL* .

Cheers, and hoping to see some great participation!

- Epoch Team & Tinkerer's Lab Team

3/5/23, 11:04 PM - Abhinav Kompella: Hey everyone,

We are thrilled to announce that Turing Hut, the coding club of VNR VJIET is conducting a national-level coding contest - *TURING CUP*. The contest is designed to test your coding skills, creativity, and problem-solving abilities.

The contest will be conducted in three rounds. The first round will be an online round conducted on 11th March, 2023. The second round and the third round will be held on-site on 25th March 2023, which will be conducted in the VNR VJIET campus, Hyderabad. Accommodation will be provided for teams whose college is not located in Hyderabad.

The contest is open to all the undergraduate students from across the country who are passionate about coding. We encourage you to participate in the contest and showcase your talent.

To participate in the contest, you need to register yourself at Unstop. The registration for the first round will be open until March 8th, 2023. The first round will be conducted online, and the registered participants will receive further instructions via email.

We urge you to register for the contest and showcase your coding skills to the nation. It's an excellent opportunity for you to learn, network, and grow in your career.

To know more: https://turinghut.org/turingcup
Register here: https://unstop.com/o/ue5gaLR?lb=MF8vPuG

Happy coding,
Team Turing Hut.

3/22/23, 6:19 PM - +91 85780 01808: Join Our Design and Coding Challenge and Win an Exclusive Interview Opportunity | Buildfast

Hi Coders,

We are excited to announce our Web Component Coding Competition, designed exclusively for students like you who are passionate about designing and web development. This competition is a great opportunity for you to showcase your skills and win an interview at a leading startup.

Eligibility:
All Undergrad students who are enthusiastic in Web design/FrontEnd and are currently enrolled in a recognized institution are eligible to participate in this competition.

Competition Details:
The competition involves designing and developing a web component from scratch, which make website development easier and more efficient. The web component can be developed using HTML, CSS, Javascript, and should be compatible with modern browsers. 

Duration: 3 days(6 April 2023 to 9 April 2023 till midnight)

Prizes:
The top three winners will receive a direct interview opportunity at our partner startup, which could be the beginning of an exciting career in tech and, the next top 5 candidates will receive certificate of appreciation. Our partner startups include Ninety-eight entertainment, dreate.Xr, A Design guy 

Judges and Evaluation Criteria:
The entries will be judged by our partner companies' Head of Design and Development team lead. These experts in the field of web design and development will be evaluating the entries based on the following criteria:
* Creativity: How unique and innovative is the web component?
* UI/UX feasibility: Does the web component work as intended and solve the problem it was designed for?
* Coding Best Practices: Are coding best practices followed, including maintainability, readability, and scalability?
* Number of views: No. of views your component gets after it is made live.

Register here:
To participate in the competition, please submit your entry on  https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSczraBvcqAwdEsZyJgktCRH0-FBnhdAeZRsPcieeLxAlel0bQ/viewform by 5 April 2023.

We hope that you will participate in this exciting competition and showcase your web development skills. If you have any questions or clarifications, please do not hesitate to reach out to us at uday@buildfast.co.in We wish you all the best of luck

Regards,
Uday Agarwal
Buildfast Team
